## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="d0a5b-1703">Commenti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d0a5b-1703">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d0a5b-1704">La classe **MS-DFSR-ReplicationGroup** fa parte del supporto del servizio di replica file System distribuito (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d0a5b-1704">The **ms-DFSR-ReplicationGroup** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
